102a7(phal chen): nges pa rab kyi rdul shin tu za ba snyed ni yang dag par nges pa'i phung po la rab tu 'god do// sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu za ba sbed ni dgo ba dang
102a8(phal chen): yid du 'ong ba dang / mthongs su skye ba la rab tu 'god ngo do// sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu tha basbed na/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyis la rab tu
102b1(phal chen): 'god do// sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed ni dge ba'i bshes pa shes gnyen bsnyen bkur bya ba'i bsod nams kyi tshogs la rab tu 'god do// zhing de
102b2(phal chen): dag re rer yang sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed ni/ sngan chad ma bskyed pa'i byang chub kyi sems skye bar byed do// zhing de dag re rer yang sems can
102b3(phal chen): ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa phyir mi ldog par yang dag par 'thob pa la yang dag par skul lo// zhing de dag re rer yang sems
102b4(phal chen): can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi spyan chos thams cad kun nas snang zhing gzigs pa la yongs su spangs te rab tu 'god do//
102b5(phal chen): zhing du de dag re rer yang sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed stobs thams cad kyis rab tu gnas pa dang / ye shes kyi tshogs zad mi shes pa dang / sangs rgyas

197a6(phal chen): dbyangs te// 'jig rten kun gyi dbyangs su yang // la la'i zhing na rab tu grag/ zhing rnams la la sprin gyi sgra// ron chen rgya mtsho'i 'od zer dang // nor bu'i shing gi gzugs sgra dang /

209b1(phal chen): can/ sangs rgyas byang chub smon lam yang dag gnas// sems can kun gyi mgon dang gnas gyur pa'i// rgyal ba dam pa bsam gyis mi khyab 'gyur// ye shes rgya mtsho chen po

222a3(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor dang ldan pa yod de/ der skad cig skad cig tu de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul/
222a4(phal chen): shin du phra ba sred mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya mapas de'i phyir gling byang chub kyi rgyal mtshan de la/ byang chub kyi rgyal mtshan zhes bya'o// de ltar de dag la sogs pa gling byang chub
222a5(phal chen): kyi rgyal mtshan de ni/ yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan pa ste/ mdor na gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams gnas kyi dam pa de na/ yon tan byang chub gang ji snyed yod pa'i yan tan
222a6(phal chen): de dag ni/ gling byang chub kyi rgyal mtshan de na yod do// gling byang chub kyi rgyal mtshan de na/ grong rdal mdzod mtha' yas pa zhes bya/ khang pa brdzogs pa'i dbyibs su 'dug pa/
222a7(phal chen): grod rdul 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu rtsu bskyed hU~M 'khor dang ldan pa yang de/ grong rdul mdzod patha' yas pa zhes bya ba den/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dngong/
222a8(phal chen): pa'i phyir rgyam tsho 'dzi rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul yin du phra ba sang bu su mtshogs pa dang ldan pa'o// de bzhin gagags pa'i dgongs pa'i phyir rgya mtshar shing ma na
222b1(phal chen): 'dzin gyi 'obs rgya mtsho/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis yongs su bskor ba'o// ting nge 'dzin gyi 'obs rgya mtsho de dag re re zhing yang de bzhin gshegs pa
222b2(phal chen): zhi gnas kyi chu rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis yongs su gang ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhi gnas kyi chu rgya mtsho de dag re re zhing yang de bzhin
222b3(phal chen): gshegs pa'i ye shes dang / yon ngan gyi me tog ud pa la dang / pad+ma dang / ku mu da dang / pun da ri ka 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba snyed kyis kun nas
222b4(phal chen): khyab par gang ba'o// grong rdal mdzod mtha' yas pa de na/ byang chub kyi sems rin po che shin tu rnam par dag pa'i pha gu ma rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin
222b5(phal chen): du phra ba snyed las brtsigs pa/ sa bcu'i khang pa brtsegs pa dang / gzhal med khang gi phreng ba rgya mtsho/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis rje
222b6(phal chen): par phye ba ste/ grong rdal mdzod mtha' yas pa der/ sems can gang ji snyed skyes pa de dag thams cad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdza kyi chos kun gyi sku dang /
222b7(phal chen): ngang tshul rgya mtsho la rab tu zhugs pa/ skad cig skad cig cing sems can gyi khams sna tshogs/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba snyed yongs su mya ngan las
222b8(phal chen): zlo bla 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho sna tshogs/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung po rgya mtsho'i khur/ 'jig rten gyi khams
223a1(phal chen): rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bkur ba la yongs su skyo ba med pa sha stag go/ ci'i phyir grong rdal mdzod batha' yas pa zhes bya ba de la mdzod
223a2(phal chen): mtha' yas pa zhes bya ba zhe na/ grong rdal mdzod mtha' yas pa de'i sa'i khams kyi rdul shin du phra ba 'am/ chu'i khams kyi rdul shin du phra ba 'am/ me'i khams kyi rdul shin
223a3(phal chen): du za ba 'am/ rlung gi khams kyi rdul yin du phra ba 'am/ nam mkha'i khams kyi rdul shin du phra ba yang rung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis de dag la chos kyi mdzad
223a4(phal chen): mcho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba sbed ma bzhag pa/ de lta bu gang yang med pas/ de'i phyir grong rdal mdzod mtha' yas pa de la mdzod mtha' yas pa zhes bya'o// de ltar de /
223a5(phal chen): lha sogs pa slong rdal mdzong mtha' yas pa de ni/ yon tam tshar med pa dang ldan pa ste/ mngar na gling byang chub kyi rgyal mtshan na/ yon tan gang ji snyed yang ba'i yon tan
223a6(phal chen): snong na/ grong rdal mdzod mtha' yas pa rer mdzo// grong rdal mtshar mdza' yas pa dzin/ bza' shing ga rab mya ngam dang bral ba zhes bya ba snang pa byang chub ma ngang med
223a7(phal chen): pa'i dbyibs su 'dug pa/ bza' shing gyi ba 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du zla ba snyed kyi 'khor dang ldan pa yod de/ bza' shing gI ba mya ngam da
223a8(phal chen): ba den/ nags tshal rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba snying yo de/ nags tshal de dag kyang so so nas stong pa nyid kyi gser rgya mtsho 'dzim
223a9(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams

223b2(phal chen): ldan pa'o// rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen po rgya mtsho/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'bras bu dang ldan pa'o// sems can gyi khams
223b3(phal chen): thams cad sdig pa las yongs su skyob pa rgya mtsho/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba sred kyi lo ma dang ldan pa'o// sems can gyi khams yongs
223b4(phal chen): su mya ngan las zlo ba rgya mtsho/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba sred kyi grib ma bsil ba dang ldan pa'o// sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi
223b5(phal chen): bsam pa'i sa rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya margya bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba snyed la snying po'i rtsa ba rab tu gnas pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad ye
223b6(phal chen): shes gang chen mtsho'i sngon gyi smon lam rgya mtsho/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi yal ga dang ldan pa'o// rang bzhin yongs su dag pa'i
223b7(phal chen): dar gyi lda ldi dang / chun po rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kun tu bres pa'o// dri ma med cing yongs su dag pa'i gdugs dang / rgyal
223b8(phal chen): mtshan dang / bdan/ rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba snyed mngon par bsgreng ba'o// bza' shing gi ra ba mya ngan dang bral ba de ni rdzing rgya mtsho
224a1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba snyed kyis yongs su brgyan pa ste/ rdzing de dag re re zhing yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhi gnas rgya mtshan
224a2(phal chen): chu 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba snyed kyis yongs su gang ba'o// rdzing de dag re re zhing yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes dang / yon tan gyi me matog ud

224a4(phal chen): ji snyed cig 'dongad pa de dag thams cad kyang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad ye shes gang chen mtsho'i sku dang thugs dpa' phrin las mnyam pa rgya
224a5(phal chen): mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba sred rab tu thob par gyur pa sha stag go/ dus gsum pa thams cad du thogs pa med pa'i ye shes la rnam par spyad/

224a7(phal chen): zhe na/ shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams mya ngan dang bral ba zhes bya ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa mya ngan dang bral ba zhes bya ba bzhugs te/ de dang 'thun pa'i rgyus grus
224a8(phal chen): pas/ de'i phyir na bza' shing rab mya ngan dang bral ba de la mya ngan dang bral ba zhes bya'o// de dag la sogs pa bza' shing gir bya mya ngan dang bral ba de ni yon tan

227b6(phal chen): lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang mi dang mi ma yin pa rgya mtsho ji snyed cig yod pa de dag thams cad la yongs su bskul ba byed
227b7(phal chen): do/ shar phyogs dang 'dra bar phyogs phyogs kyi rgya mtsho thams cad du yang de bzhin te/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho de dag dang / mi dang mi ma yin rgya mtsho
227b8(phal chen): snyed pa de dag/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes gang chen mtsho rnam par snang mdzad kyi 'od zer gyis yang dag par skul nas/ rang rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing
228a1(phal chen): rgya mtsho dag na/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho ji snyed gang bzhugs pa de dag la zhus te/ gang nas byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho re dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa
228a2(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i bar de dag re re zhing yang byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor rgya mtsho nas/ mi dang mi ma yin pa'i 'khor rgya mtsho'i bar dang ldan par 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
228a3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag gi 'thil gyi snying po la rab tu gnas pa gang na ba der 'dong bar gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho de dag dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa
228a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i bar de dag la/ byang chub sems dpa' ji srid cig yod pa dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa ji snyed cig yod pa de dag las/ byang chub sems dpa' re re dang /
228a5(phal chen): mi dang mi ma yin pa'i bar de dag re re zhing yang lus rgya mtsho/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba snyed dang ldan pa sha stag ste/ lus re re la yang la

229a3(phal chen): dge ba'i chos don bzang po// yi ge bzang po// dag pa yongs su gsal ba/ yongs su byang ba/ tshangs pa'i spyong ba yang dag par ston cing / byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten

229a8(phal chen): dupra bsnyed kyis dus gsum rgya mche/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin du phra ba skad du gsungs te/ bstan kyang zad par mi rung // 'jig rten gyi khams

229b8(phal chen): yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che rgya mtsho dang / nam mkha' rgyan gyis 'gengs pa'i gdugs rin po che rgya mtsho dang / rang bzhin gyis dri ma med pa'i gos rin po che rgya mtsho dang / zla ba'i
